  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2bf1c5de-cf3b-481d-bb48-145a12c2d0f6'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer16505525599732691840"><b>She's about to walk on the wild side . . . </b><br/><br/>While filling the display case in her bakery, the bell over the door sounds and Tessa O'Hara looks up to see the man of her dreams.   <span id="freeText16505525599732691840" style="display:none"><b>She's about to walk on the wild side . . . </b><br /><br />While filling the display case in her bakery, the bell over the door sounds and Tessa O'Hara looks up to see the man of her dreams. Within thirty seconds he asks her out for a beer. But after four months of dating, she discovers he's an undercover DEA agent-and he's investigating her possible role in her ex-husband's drug business. For Tess, this means their relationship is over. <br /><br />Brock disagrees. He's committed to his anti-drug mission, but he's fallen in love with the beautiful woman who's as sweet as her cupcakes-and he'll do anything to win her back. Standing between Tess and Brock are their own exes, one of them a drug lord who's determined to get what he wants. Now as danger threatens, can Brock break the rules he's lived by and let loose his wild side to protect the woman he loves?</span>
  <a data-text-id="16505525599732691840" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

<div id="review_283228614" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/283228614" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/283228614?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-ebook-borrowed">format-ebook-borrowed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-dream-man">series-dream-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=im-a-kristen-ashley-ho">im-a-kristen-ashley-ho</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer283228614" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8222507749987836331"><blockquote>
  <a href='http://s385.photobucket.com/user/ohbleep/media/Misc/0221a051-dc12-4ab6-8bd1-ad61a57bc434_zpsc433f934.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384738942i/6951783.jpg' alt=' photo 0221a051-dc12-4ab6-8bd1-ad61a57bc434_zpsc433f934.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  </a>
</blockquote>I usually hate sounding like a broken record, but I've decided that sometimes, it's not a bad thing. And in this case, book after book, review after review of saying the same things, I’m beginning to think that Kristen Ashley can write no wrong. I’ve read five of her books, back-to-back, and while this is going to sound wonky, I’m not looking forward to reading her entire back-list because then I’ll have read her entire back-list and will have to wait for new releases and I just can’</span>
  <span id="freeText8222507749987836331" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s385.photobucket.com/user/ohbleep/media/Misc/0221a051-dc12-4ab6-8bd1-ad61a57bc434_zpsc433f934.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384738942i/6951783.jpg" alt=" photo 0221a051-dc12-4ab6-8bd1-ad61a57bc434_zpsc433f934.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote>I usually hate sounding like a broken record, but I've decided that sometimes, it's not a bad thing. And in this case, book after book, review after review of saying the same things, I’m beginning to think that Kristen Ashley can write no wrong. I’ve read five of her books, back-to-back, and while this is going to sound wonky, I’m not looking forward to reading her entire back-list because then I’ll have read her entire back-list and will have to wait for new releases and I just can’t imagine that that will be very much fun. The waiting, that is. <br><br>So here we go, breakin’ it down:<br><br>What I loved:<br><br>1.	Brock Lucas is what you’d call an alpha male. Not just a little alpha, but uber alpha, as in over the top, nigh unto crazy alpha, which makes him not just amazing, but All. Kinds. Of. Amazing.<br><br>2.	Tessa O’Hare is a fantastic heroine. Not whiney, not clingy, and definitely not stupid. She’s smart, mature, savvy, talented, loving, devoted…. The list goes on and on, but most importantly, she loves Brock and so I love her.<br><br>3.	Brocks family – pain in the asses every one, but also all kinds of awesome. It’s a Lucas family thing, I’m sure.<br><br>4.	EMOTIONAL story! Loved it. Couldn’t get enough of it. Hated for it to end.<br><br>What I didn’t love:<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s385.photobucket.com/user/ohbleep/media/Misc/3ca13808-9f73-48ae-8836-7df78ebbcc9b_zpsa9cb6f82.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384739667i/6952551.jpg" alt=" photo 3ca13808-9f73-48ae-8836-7df78ebbcc9b_zpsa9cb6f82.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote>So there ya have it! Another fantastic, sexy, exciting, awesome story by Kristen Ashley!!<br><br>-----<br>If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br><br></span>

<div id="review_381179420" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/381179420" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381179420?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381179420" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18425903666604271106"><b>5 WILD stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/f5b0dca5-b96c-4287-b76f-adfefdfff1ed_zps33abcb4b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384658834i/6926170.jpg' alt=' photo f5b0dca5-b96c-4287-b76f-adfefdfff1ed_zps33abcb4b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I love the Dream Man series. I read Mystery Man and I loved it. I fell in love with Tack, so I skipped right over Wild Man and Law Man and jumped right into Motorcycle Man(this was back in February). I spent the last few days listening to the audiobook of Wild Man. Why the hell haven’t I read this before??? I wish I would have went back to this sooner... it was great! <br/><br/><br/>Tessa O’Hara is the owner of a bakery. Brock Lucas is a DEA agent. They meet under less than ideal circumstances</span>
  <span id="freeText18425903666604271106" style="display:none"><b>5 WILD stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/f5b0dca5-b96c-4287-b76f-adfefdfff1ed_zps33abcb4b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384658834i/6926170.jpg" alt=" photo f5b0dca5-b96c-4287-b76f-adfefdfff1ed_zps33abcb4b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I love the Dream Man series. I read Mystery Man and I loved it. I fell in love with Tack, so I skipped right over Wild Man and Law Man and jumped right into Motorcycle Man(this was back in February). I spent the last few days listening to the audiobook of Wild Man. Why the hell haven’t I read this before??? I wish I would have went back to this sooner... it was great! <br><br><br>Tessa O’Hara is the owner of a bakery. Brock Lucas is a DEA agent. They meet under less than ideal circumstances. Brock is investigating her ex-husband, who is a drug dealer. Brock is undercover at the beginning of their relationship. It was the best few months of ‘work’ he’s ever had. When Tess finds out who Brock really is, she doesn’t take it that way. She’s not very happy. But she understands after a while. Brock and Tess are amazing together, but with her ex-husband and his bitchy and crazy ex-wife, things aren’t always easy for them. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a210021b-118a-4767-bbab-13ed64a381b9_zps9eba7181.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384658834i/6926171.jpg" alt=" photo a210021b-118a-4767-bbab-13ed64a381b9_zps9eba7181.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brock and Tess... Brock is my kinda KA alpha. Hot, protective, sweet, sexy, possessive. All the best qualities in a man! As much as I loved him, Tess was really the shining star in this book! What a fantastic heroine! She was too sweet, with the perfect amount of sass and zero annoying qualities! I loved the way she was with Brock’s family, her strength and courage blew me away. <br><br><b>♥ ♥ ♥ Some of my favorite quotes ♥ ♥ ♥ </b><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Babe, you think I found the women of my dreams at 45 years old and I'm gonna let anything happen to her, think again. That's a long fuckin' time to wait for what you want. I waited. I found it. I'm pullin' out all the stops to take care of it.” <br><br>“Darlin’, the last time I walked into a mall was two presidents ago.”<br> I stared at him in shock. Then I asked, <br>“Is that even possible?”<br> “I got a dick and I was single so, yeah, it’s possible.” <br><br>When my phone rang at the bakery, this usually meant someone wanted to order a birthday cake. When Brock’s rang at the Station, this usually meant someone had a cap busted in their ass. My job was WAY better.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>And that epilogue! That has to be one of the best KA epilogues ever. I’m not sure if I was in emotional state of mind while reading, or what but I cried like a baby through the whole thing! It was just too good, too beautiful! This book was amazing. Yep! I know one thing for sure, I will not be waiting 8 months to read Law Man like I did this- I’ll be getting to Detective Mitch Lawson’s book soon!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/3604cc3c-45ca-48eb-a598-a3a5120cda80_zps9bed8002.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384658834i/6926172.jpg" alt=" photo 3604cc3c-45ca-48eb-a598-a3a5120cda80_zps9bed8002.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/280350967?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cop-hero">cop-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=lost-love-rekindled">lost-love-rekindled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280350967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17576258466253668077">I’m moving to Colorado. Being a Brit, I’m not entirely sure I know where it is exactly. Up from Texas, in the middle, left a bit?? Anyway, I’m definitely going because, according to Kristen Ashley, it is packed to the rafters with Mega Hot Uber-Alpha guys just waiting to be snapped up by their forever girl. Now, where’s that green card application………………….<br/><br/>So Wild Man – this is Brock Lucas who we first met working undercover as a DEA Agent back in Mystery Man. He’s again working undercover trying </span>
  <span id="freeText17576258466253668077" style="display:none">I’m moving to Colorado. Being a Brit, I’m not entirely sure I know where it is exactly. Up from Texas, in the middle, left a bit?? Anyway, I’m definitely going because, according to Kristen Ashley, it is packed to the rafters with Mega Hot Uber-Alpha guys just waiting to be snapped up by their forever girl. Now, where’s that green card application………………….<br /><br />So Wild Man – this is Brock Lucas who we first met working undercover as a DEA Agent back in Mystery Man. He’s again working undercover trying to bring down Damian Heller by schmoozing up to his ex-wife Tess. He realises very early on that his feelings for Tess are real and not part of his Op but can’t tell her. Tess gets hauled in for questioning in the dead of the night, she’s innocent of course, and spots Brock, Jake as she’s known him, in full DEA gear and feels betrayed. Brock gives her some time and then goes after her and they resume their relationship pretty quickly, this time openly and honestly.<br /><br />Tess has to be one of my favourite Kristen Ashley heroines – she’s open, engaging, without guile and as sweet as the cakes she bakes for a living. Brock is typical KA Hero Fare – he’s bossy, protective, possessive, domineering but also caring and tender – I loved him. He’s got a big conflicted family, a picture perfect hard as nails shallow ex-wife and 2 lovely boys. What I liked most about him was how he loved and cherished Tess – he genuinely adored her, worried about her and was beside himself when she was taken from him and he called her My Sweet Tess. Tess is absolutely perfect for him - she talks so much sense and is so loyal to him and he knows he has a good thing here and works hard to turn things around from their rocky beginnings.<br /><br />As always, the course of true love never did run smooth and Brock’s ex, Tess’s ex and a blast from the past all conspire to throw a spanner in the works and we wouldn’t want it any other way would we?? <br /><br />It’s good to see Elvira back in action and large as life, Rock Chicks Shirleen and Daisy turn up and do their thing and we have the delightful and delicious additions of Vance and Hector who are my most favourite guys from the drooltastic Hot Bunch!<br /><br />Another sizzling hot sexy romance from Kristen Ashley<br /><br />4.5 stars – contemporary romance<br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/262373378?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=great-ending">great-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-heroine">fabulous-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characters">fabulous-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=abuse-and-or-rape-issues">abuse-and-or-rape-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characterizations">fabulous-characterizations</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer262373378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8606303032224203507"><b>
  <u>Solid 4 stars</u>
</b><br/><br/>I really enjoyed reading <i>Wild Man</i>; however, it didn't capture and hold my attention like I hoped it would. What I did like about this book was the engaging, sensually passionate, and realistic relationship between the hero and heroine, Tess and Brock. Tess's character, though, is what made this book shine. She was simply fabulous! I admired her straightforwardness and simple honesty. She didn't play games with Brock. She told him exactly what she felt, thought, and wanted. She w</span>
  <span id="freeText8606303032224203507" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Solid 4 stars</u>
</b><br /><br />I really enjoyed reading <i>Wild Man</i>; however, it didn't capture and hold my attention like I hoped it would. What I did like about this book was the engaging, sensually passionate, and realistic relationship between the hero and heroine, Tess and Brock. Tess's character, though, is what made this book shine. She was simply fabulous! I admired her straightforwardness and simple honesty. She didn't play games with Brock. She told him exactly what she felt, thought, and wanted. She was open, honest, and caring. Her character was a breath of fresh air and I adored her. <br /><br />For some reason, Brock's character didn't leave a huge impression or have much impact on me. Not like the other Kristen Ashley heroes have. I really liked him, don't get me wrong, but he never fully came to life for me. When he was with Tess, however, they were magical. <br /><br />The secondary characters were fleshed out, humorous, and very entertaining. Brock's family was a bit over-the-top for me, but I still got a kick out of them. I really liked Tess's relationship with her girlfriends. Once again, Kristen Ashley creates magic. <i>Wild Man</i> is a sexy, heartwarming, and entertaining book. One I highly recommend.<br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8606303032224203507" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416700443?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/19082465-wild-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=a-re-read">a-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416700443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8787745894212751171"><b>
  <i>My wild is a safe place for you...</i>
</b><br/><br/>Nothing to add besides what I added to the narrator section of the review. My heart was broken when Daisy hit the scene...because it didn't sound like <i>my</i> Daisy. I think, with all the other narrators giving her a twang and a bit of personality, I just expect it. No *Sugar* or *Bunches of Love* that I've come to expect and love. Obviously, it wasn't in for the narrator to say, but I missed it. This narrator just doesn't do her justice, unfortunately. <br/><br/>The story</span>
  <span id="freeText8787745894212751171" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>My wild is a safe place for you...</i>
</b><br /><br />Nothing to add besides what I added to the narrator section of the review. My heart was broken when Daisy hit the scene...because it didn't sound like <i>my</i> Daisy. I think, with all the other narrators giving her a twang and a bit of personality, I just expect it. No *Sugar* or *Bunches of Love* that I've come to expect and love. Obviously, it wasn't in for the narrator to say, but I missed it. This narrator just doesn't do her justice, unfortunately. <br /><br />The story is still excellent and kept my attention from start to finish.<br /><br />**********<br /><br /><b>An Audio Review</b><br /><br />My audiobooks aren’t lasting as long as they should be. I <i>was</i> buying them to keep me amused on the way to and from work and when I bake or exercise. It seems that I’m struggling to just keep it to those times. I mean, it’s hard to just limit myself. I’m invested in the story. I’ve been sucked in. There’s a crucial stage I’m reaching and the last thing I want to do is press stop and wait. This means I’m listening to nearly one a week and putting off book reading to listen instead.<br /><br />Well, this is what happened when I started <i>Wild Man</i>. I just couldn't stop. It’s a re-read, so the story isn’t new to me, but it is a KA which means it's very hard to put down. When Brock steps into a room he’s got my full attention. Tess going through a crisis because Damien (her ex-husband) is stalking her, well, of course, I need to listen to it now before I hit stop. Olivia and her bony ass making a nuisance, well, it’s got to be sorted out. This is the struggle I face. It’s tough, but someone’s got to do it.<br /><br />The beginning of <i>Wild Man</i> is a little hard to take and each re-read/listen still has that seem punch. We meet Tess and Brock after they had been in a relationship for 4 months. Tess really likes Brock and while Brock seems to like Tess, he also seems to be holding himself back a bit. This is because Brock is an undercover DEA agent, and he’s investigating Tess because of her douchewaffle ex-husband and the bugger's drug business. When Tess finds out that Brock had only approached her because of his job she’s devastated. She puts it behind her and tries to move on with her life. Brock lets her have a little time to get over it and then comes after her. <br /><br />Well, this is a KA book and of course, when you have one of her heroes chasing you, you walk away…very, very slowly, in the hopes, he’ll catch you, chuck you over his shoulder and claim you. Yes, Tess put up a token resistance, but Brock is way too much temptation to refuse.<br /><br />Their relationship is not all plain sailing. Brock has an ex-wife and two sons. The ex is a skank who treats her kids pretty shabby. Up till now, Brock hasn’t been in a position to contest custody. With the change in his job (leaving DEA to be a detective) and finally having a good woman in his life, it’s now time to try. The ex, Olivia, does not make things easy and she tries to manipulate the boys for her own gain. With Tess on the scene, Olivia has a new target to aim for.<br /><br />So, between Brock’s ex, Tess’s ex, her bakery, and his job they definitely have their hands full. It doesn’t take her long to realise that all the stress is worth it. Brock and his two boys have brought a lot of happiness to her life. Tess is the woman Brock has been waiting for and it also helps that she bakes a mean cake or cookie.<br /><br />Now, in regards to the audio, it was pretty good. The narrator's voice is easy to listen to and understand. I did have a bit of a problem when she changed from a female character to a male character as she doesn’t change her voice much. This does make it a little hard. It was more like someone just reading the story to me instead of acting it out. That probably sounds weird, acting it out, but some of the best audio’s, the narrator is able to manipulate their voice so it’s easy to hear the emotions and tell the changes in characters. My biggest complaint...she butchered my Daisy. Unfortunately, there was no twang and I just didn't get the right vibe for her. Shirleen and Elvira were definitely given more voice in this one.<br /><br /><i>Wild Man</i> is one of my favourite <i>Kristen Ashley</i> stories. For one thing, Tess mentioning Snickerdoodles, which I had never heard of before this book so made me go searching for a recipe. In my boys' circle of friends, I’m known for 1 - The biscuits that taste like cinnamon doughnuts. AND 2 - (whispers) Snickerdoodle has the word doodle in them. The smirks on their faces when they ask for a snickerdoodle is priceless. Boys and their doodles. ;)<br /><br />I’ve already got my next audio lined up and I’m hoping it will last more than a few days.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8787745894212751171" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7633932265557615473"><b>3 Stars <i>(Read 5/10/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b>DNF @ 19% <i>(8/2/2016)</i></b><br/><br/>Well, I had finished <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_' title='Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Law Man</a> not that long ago and thought I needed to go back and give this one a try. Sadly, it didn't work out so well.<br/><br/>I hated the way the h was expected to just get over what the H had done to her. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ He was an undercover DEA agent and was investigating her and her relationship with her ex (who ended up being some big drug distributor). He dated her for 4 months under a false identity, and even slept with her!  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide sp</a></span></span>
  <span id="freeText7633932265557615473" style="display:none"><b>3 Stars <i>(Read 5/10/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b>DNF @ 19% <i>(8/2/2016)</i></b><br /><br />Well, I had finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a> not that long ago and thought I needed to go back and give this one a try. Sadly, it didn't work out so well.<br /><br />I hated the way the h was expected to just get over what the H had done to her. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ He was an undercover DEA agent and was investigating her and her relationship with her ex (who ended up being some big drug distributor). He dated her for 4 months under a false identity, and even slept with her!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. She was upset about it and the H leaves her alone for 3 months and then shows up and says "you're done being mad" and then she was!! I know, I know -- it's the typical KA pushy, alpha man. But it just didn't work for me <i>AT ALL</i> in this one. I felt like he needed to do some major groveling, or at least <i>acknowledge</i> how hurtful his behavior was. <br /><br />I also didn't like that we start the book already into their relationship. I like to experience the development of feelings, and both the h and H seem to already have strong feelings from the start.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> is one of my favorites, so I won't be quitting on her now...but I just have to pass on finishing this one.<br /><br /><b>**5/10/2019 Update**</b><br /><br />I needed an audiobook to listen to and this book came up. I've had some pretty decent success with Kristen Ashley books as audiobooks in the past and even though I couldn't even finish this the first time, I thought "why not?" and gave it another shot. I was in the mood for some old school KA especially after (the train wreck that was) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/44102654.The_Slow_Burn__Moonlight_and_Motor_Oil___2_" title="The Slow Burn (Moonlight and Motor Oil, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Slow Burn</a>. After listening to this enough (and I think the audiobook delivery made it more tolerable too) to get past the cringeworthy beginning and what bothered me so much the first time I read it, I downloaded this ebook from my library to start reading. I won't lie. I still had some major issues with how they were reunited. I skimmed a good bit because of it. I still didn't like how the H didn't really grovel and just told her to "move on" without really acknowledging that he did something hurtful. It also had a lot of OW/OM drama that I know other people don't like (their exes), but honestly doesn't bother me too much. Otherwise, this had the old KA vibe that I was looking for with the bevy of side characters/family and the right amount of suspense to keep me interested. I still struggled, it's not going down as one of my favorites -- but I got through it and I didn't really hate it either...so I'm going with middle of the road 3 Stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7633932265557615473" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4379929522984397075"><b>What I liked: </b><br/><br/><b>1.</b> Tess owning a bakery. <br/><b>2.</b> Brock.<br/><b>3.</b> Brock and Tess's relationship. It was cheesy but beautiful.<br/><br/><b>What I disliked:</b><br/><br/><b>1.</b> The beginning was slow and it took me nearly 40% to truly get into the story.<br/><b>2.</b> Brock acting like every other hero of KA's with very few distinguishing characteristics. <br/><b>3.</b> Tessa being a curvy blonde in her forties. Brunettes and redheads in their twenties or early thirties clearly don't exist in KAland. <br/><b>4.</b> The writing. I know I should be getting used to it with each KA</span>
  <span id="freeText4379929522984397075" style="display:none"><b>What I liked: </b><br /><br /><b>1.</b> Tess owning a bakery. <br /><b>2.</b> Brock.<br /><b>3.</b> Brock and Tess's relationship. It was cheesy but beautiful.<br /><br /><b>What I disliked:</b><br /><br /><b>1.</b> The beginning was slow and it took me nearly 40% to truly get into the story.<br /><b>2.</b> Brock acting like every other hero of KA's with very few distinguishing characteristics. <br /><b>3.</b> Tessa being a curvy blonde in her forties. Brunettes and redheads in their twenties or early thirties clearly don't exist in KAland. <br /><b>4.</b> The writing. I know I should be getting used to it with each KA book I read, but the opposite's happening. I'm increasingly disliking the way her characters talk and narrate.<br /><b>5.</b> The run-on sentences and never-ending paragraphs. I know this could fit in #4, but it deserves its own number because of how much it bugged me. <br /><br /><b>What I loved:</b><br /><br /><b>1.</b> Levi and Lenore's relationship.<br /><b>2.</b> The ending, of course.<br /><br /><b>For more reviews, visit my <a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/&lt;br /&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>.</b></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

<div id="review_819786705" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/819786705" />
    <a title="Raine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27288811-raine"><img alt="Raine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416553295p2/27288811.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/819786705?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Raine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Raine" href="/user/show/27288811-raine">Raine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18889012-wild-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=erotica-contemporary">erotica-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=0-read-2016">0-read-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=zz_2016-dhasg-yearly-challenge">zz_2016-dhasg-yearly-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=0-read-2017">0-read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=0-read-2015">0-read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=police">police</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27288811-raine?shelf=erotica-suspense-mystery-thriller">erotica-suspense-mystery-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer819786705" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1822461776328410068"><b>Slim is the sh**!!!</b><br/><br/>Why do I not have a review for this book??? I LOVE this book and have read it over 5 times. <br/><br/>While this is not my top favorite of Kristen Ashley books (Rock Chick Regret #7 takes that #1 spot) it is still one of my favorites to re-read. After every re-read of a book I always look at the number of stars I had given it previously and think if I should change it and NEVER have I thought twice to lower the star count from 5, so hopefully that should say something about this book. <br/><br/>B</span>
  <span id="freeText1822461776328410068" style="display:none"><b>Slim is the sh**!!!</b><br /><br />Why do I not have a review for this book??? I LOVE this book and have read it over 5 times. <br /><br />While this is not my top favorite of Kristen Ashley books (Rock Chick Regret #7 takes that #1 spot) it is still one of my favorites to re-read. After every re-read of a book I always look at the number of stars I had given it previously and think if I should change it and NEVER have I thought twice to lower the star count from 5, so hopefully that should say something about this book. <br /><br />Brock "Slim" Lucas is a DEA agent and was tasked with investigating and tailing Tessa O'Hara. She gets caught up in this drama, but learns to forgive Brock and they start their relationship. I love that they stick together and are together from the beginning of the book to the end despite their drama with their respective families - Brock with his crazy ex-wife and kids and Tessa with her criminal ex-husband. <br /><br />At the beginning of the book you may think 'Man, Tessa just forgave Brock right away and she should have given him a little more shit about it.' But as you read more you realize that Tessa is not a pushover. She is really a strong character to be able to forgive him for his deceit in the beginning of the book and take all the drama that is their family and STILL bake awesome cupcakes with mountainous swirls of frosting. I like reading the story from Tessa's POV, her head is a nice place to be...not too much drama and not too angsty, but still very insightful. When I grow up I wanna be her!<br /><br />Now Brock, he is an alpha who uses a lot of four letter words even in front of his kids, but he tells it how it is and doesn't do it eloquently, but with a lot of no apology attitude. And the dirty talk...every time he opens his mouth I feel like I just melt into a big wet puddle!<br /><br />*****Re-read again for about the 8th time! Still love it!!!*****<br />NOTE: Last re-read on 8/16/2015<br /><br />*****Re-read again for about the 9th time*****<br />NOTE: Last re-read on 6/26/2016</span>
  <a data-text-id="1822461776328410068" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/332272565?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer332272565" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18204865104935838315">4.5 stars<br/><br/><i> <b> "I can't make any promises about where this is gonna go but what I can do is give you me, keep you safe while you walk on the wild side and work my ass off to do what I can so this never goes bad for you." </b></i>  ~Brock Lucas<br/><br/>Oooo Kristen Ashley does it again! I loved Brock and Tess' story! I loved how FUNCTIONAL they were as a couple!! Its always SO refreshing to find book couples like that. Ones who talk through their issues, don't let stupid things come between them and are open and hone</span>
  <span id="freeText18204865104935838315" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br><br><i> <b> "I can't make any promises about where this is gonna go but what I can do is give you me, keep you safe while you walk on the wild side and work my ass off to do what I can so this never goes bad for you." </b></i>  ~Brock Lucas<br><br>Oooo Kristen Ashley does it again! I loved Brock and Tess' story! I loved how FUNCTIONAL they were as a couple!! Its always SO refreshing to find book couples like that. Ones who talk through their issues, don't let stupid things come between them and are open and honest with each other.<br><br><i> "No games, no lies, no bullshit." </i><br><br>It was different than book 1, less action-packed, more focused on relationship development, and family drama. But as usual, it was filled with yummy, hot, swoon/drool-worthy alpha men, strong heroines, and an engaging plotline.<br><br>Brock Lucas is a DEA agent that we originally met in book 1, Mystery Man. In the beginning of the story, his job is to get close to Tess O'Hara to discover any possible connection to her ex-husband's dirty business deals. But he soon falls for her and realizes she's completely not involved and they begin a 4 month relationship but with her only knowing him under his work alias. When she is brought in for questioning in relation to her ex-husband's case, he (listening in on the interview) discovers that she was raped by her ex and looses it. But she sees him at the station, realizes that he was part of the case the whole time and doesn't want to see him again. Three months later, after giving her space to heal, Brock shows up and in his typical, no-bullshit, we-will-deal-with-this-properly attitude, demands she listen to him and hear his side of the story. The combination of her being reasonable and him not playing games and being completely honest about things leads them into a beautiful relationship.<br><br><i> "Brock Lucas is wild and he's rough and he's driven but he's loving and affectionate and so fucking loyal it isn't funny. He takes care of me. He make's me feel safe..." </i><br><br>I loved how instantly and whole-heartedly Tess accepted Brock's 2 sons into her life. Between her monster of an ex-husband and his crazy ex-wife, they have a lot of family drama to deal with but they never let anything come between them, and if anything, everything just makes them come together closer as a family unit.<br><br>I loved how caring, protective and understanding Brock was about Tess' past. She was raped by her ex-husband and was obviously quite scarred by the experience. But he helps her learn to trust again, and deal with her emotions, and heal by creating a relationship she can feel absolutely safe in.<br><br><i> "Babe, he took your power. Tonight, you took it back. And it..." his arm gave me a squeeze, "was," his hand gave me a squeeze, "fuckin'," his forehead dropped to rest on mine, " beautiful."<br><br>I closed my eyes and pulled in a deep breath.<br><br>Then I opened them and said, "You had my back."<br><br>"I always have your back." </i><br><br>I loved seeing all the factions of characters from Kristen Ashley's world working together. Lee Nightingale's boys (from the Rock Chick series), Hawk's commandos (from book 1), and Brock and Mitch's cops make for delicious additions to the story.<br><br>And I loved how in the end, when the shit hit the fan, Tess was no damsel in distress and you could really see the healing that she went through in action.<br><br>Here's how I see Brock and Tess:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378163i/733615._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, come visit my book blog at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/">http://aestasbookblog.com/</a><br><br>Or come join my FB group: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18204865104935838315" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6348724228695399708">This was such a wonderfull read :) Although in the Dream Man series this one always comes last whenever there are comparisons, after reading it again, I really don't know why, it was just incredible! I think I liked it more now than when I first read it.<br/><br/>For starters, I LOVED the fact that they are both older. They're mature, don't fight about stupid shit, they have a problem, they work it out. Aside the one big fight they had at the beginning, that was it. Always something happening, and they al</span>
  <span id="freeText6348724228695399708" style="display:none">This was such a wonderfull read :) Although in the Dream Man series this one always comes last whenever there are comparisons, after reading it again, I really don't know why, it was just incredible! I think I liked it more now than when I first read it.<br /><br />For starters, I LOVED the fact that they are both older. They're mature, don't fight about stupid shit, they have a problem, they work it out. Aside the one big fight they had at the beginning, that was it. Always something happening, and they always worked it through together. There were no plays, on either sides, they both knew what they wanted and they got it :) I think Brock and Tess are one of my favorite couples EVER! They show maturity, one partner supporting the other during some pretty terrible emotional times, helpes her heal and move on with her life. They don't keep secrets from each other, something happens - they lay it out in the open. They dissagree - they fight - they work it out - they make up. No bullshit round it. And that's what I really loved. This is a perfect example of a highly functioning couple, and how you can have 500 pages of a healthy relationship, and it still remains interesting from page 1 to the end. Just great writing. </span>

He seemed to have calmed down in this book.   <span id="freeText5033573350917275697" style="display:none">I'm a bit surprised with how much I loved Brock. I did not like him in book 1 because he was too careless with the heroine in that book. He seemed to have calmed down in this book. Add to the fact that he never had a jerk moment towards Tess, which is rare for a KA book, he turned out way better than I was expecting.<br /><br />Both characters were enjoyable. No jerk moments and not a ton of pushing away that would have had me wanting to shake someone. I like that Brock's kids were in this and there were great moments Tess had with them.<br /><br />Both exes were a thorn in the side but overall, I think it was handled very well by both main characters. I can see re-reading this one so it was easy to give it 5 stars.<br /><br />I listened to the audiobook which had the same narrator as the first book. I'm impressed with how she actually sounded like a different character vs the first book. I think she did a great job and the editing issues in book one were not issues in this book.</span>

  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>✥ This started out a bit slow and took till about 25% for me to really get into it. <br><br>✥ I didn't like that they were already in a relationship. I missed all the firsts! <br><br>✥ Hate to say it but I wish KA would switch things up, Brock and Tess sound like everyone else with the same types of friends and the same type of family. :(<br><br>✥ I really don't care for the "C" word! <br><br>✥ There is some "sensitive" subject matter but everything is in the past and the telling is not graphic.<br><br>✥ I was a bit shocked at the lack of the sex scenes...not the amount but the lack of descriptions and fade to black! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/586699.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✥ I think I sugar OD from reading this! <i>*warning - don't read if you're trying to diet!*</i><br><br>✥ I loved all the big family get togethers!<br><br>✥ I want a Levi!<br><br>✥ The last 25% was really good and as always I love her epilogues! <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/642451.gif" width="400" height="040" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>❣ "Christmas. It does shit to people."<br><br>❣ “Now, let’s go back to me bein’ like chocolate that melts in your mouth.” <br><br>❣ “Babe, you think I found the women of my dreams at 45 years old and I'm gonna let anything happen to her, think again. That's a long fuckin' time to wait for what you want. I waited. I found it. I'm pullin' out all the stops to take care of it.” </span>
  <a data-text-id="9455770667601298087" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_243257334" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243257334" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243257334?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243257334" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer318357462027722529">Tess said to Brock:<br/><b>"You're a manly, macho, rough, wild, hot guy kind of sweet but you're sweet. I'm a mountainous swirl of frosting with a moist, rich cake as my core but you're smooth, delicious dark chocolate that tastes good from the second it hits your tongue and makes you want more the minute it melts away."</b><br/><br/>Wild Man starts right off in the middle of Brock and Tess's story. Tess is having sex with "Jake", and she is totally clueless about his identity since he's working undercover as a DEA A</span>
  <span id="freeText318357462027722529" style="display:none">Tess said to Brock:<br /><b>"You're a manly, macho, rough, wild, hot guy kind of sweet but you're sweet. I'm a mountainous swirl of frosting with a moist, rich cake as my core but you're smooth, delicious dark chocolate that tastes good from the second it hits your tongue and makes you want more the minute it melts away."</b><br /><br />Wild Man starts right off in the middle of Brock and Tess's story. Tess is having sex with "Jake", and she is totally clueless about his identity since he's working undercover as a DEA Agent. He is investigating her drug dealing ex-husband and the possibility that she could be involved too. After Tess is arrested some evil stuff becomes visible, and when she knows that Brock "played" her, she decides it's over. But <i>Wild Man</i> Brock is on a mission and after three months he's back again.<br /><br />That's my main censure. Sweet Tess just took him back. Admittedly, she was upset for about…5 minutes? But I wanted him to grovel, as in <i>grovel!</i><br /><br />After a look in the mirror Tess came to the uneasy knowledge that she had no clue who she was, no clue where she was going and no clue who she wanted to be. Therefore, sweet Tess has a craving to take a walk on the wild side together with <i>Wild Man</i> Brock "Slim" Lucas. Tess is <b>scared</b> but Brock said:<br /><br /><i>"Don't be. There's a wild that's fucked and there's a wild that's just plain wild. You just hooked yourself to a different kind of wild, Tess, and I swear, baby,</i> <b>swear,</b><i>" his arms squeezed before he finished, "I'll show you that's a good, safe place to be."</i><br /><br />Brock learns all kinds of sweet things about Tess and he said:<br /><br /><i>"Tess, I learned somethin' early about you. You are the only woman I know who doesn't need words. Everything you do speaks for you and it never lies. Just your hand on me, babe, said it all."</i><br /><br />I really liked <i> the cake baking superhero</i> Tessa a lot. She didn't bitch around like other heroines and it was pretty simple. With Tessa O'Hara what you see is what you get. No games, no masks, no lies, no nothing. Just Tessa.<br /><br />The whole story revolves around the evolving relationship between Brock and Tess as well as some serious family conflicts. Brock's family is kind of crazy and Brock's ex-wife is one hell of a super bitch! As always the cast of secondary characters is great and gives this story so much more depth!<br /><br />There were a few very intense, yet very touching moments that went straight to my core. I loved the commitment that these two showed to one another. Brock knew that he got lucky to have her in his life. With that said, Tess felt the same about Brock. There were lots of true feelings and emotions involved in Wild Man. It made everything so special.<br /><br />Yeah, Brock, our <i>Wild Man</i> and Tess's <i>snake charmer</i> said all kinds of sweet things:<br /><br /><i>"I had maple buttermilk pie at dinner and chocolate cake during football but I still have a taste for somethin' sweet and the sweet I wanna eat right now is my Tess."<br /><br />"It isn't the same. You're made of sugar, Tess, and it's a given you'd eventually get it good because people like you, sweet to the core, they deserve it. What I'm sayin' is I'm glad I'm the one who gets to give it to you."</i><br /><br />In hindsight I can't believe that I put this story off for such a long time. Wild Man is another wonderful story written by the amazing storyteller Kristen Ashley!</span>
  <a data-text-id="318357462027722529" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer278771417" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16676814345856899063"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote><b>Dear Brock</b><br/><br/>You are, indeed, my favorite so far. You're probably shaking your head and wondering:favorite what? Favorite hero, of course. You probably don't understand that either, but stay with me. <br/><br/>I was a bit unsure about your actions and the undercover mission(where you really got under covers, you stud, you) and I was afraid you were just using Tessa. Luckily you weren't because she has been through so, so much. Abuse and lost wishes, and now a liar on top? I'm glad you got that sorte</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16676814345856899063" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote><b>Dear Brock</b><br /><br />You are, indeed, my favorite so far. You're probably shaking your head and wondering:favorite what? Favorite hero, of course. You probably don't understand that either, but stay with me. <br /><br />I was a bit unsure about your actions and the undercover mission(where you really got under covers, you stud, you) and I was afraid you were just using Tessa. Luckily you weren't because she has been through so, so much. Abuse and lost wishes, and now a liar on top? I'm glad you got that sorted out and quite easily, too, without too many bossy orders or controlling actions. <br /><br />I loved the slow development of your relationship with Tessa. You became her hero, her protector, her everything without being a jerk. I admire you for that. I guess it took a lot of effort to control your alpha impulses and I'm giving you your The Least Jerk badge. Congrats!!<br /><br /><i>“He ignored my push, his eyes lifted to mine and he whispered, “I can’t make any promises about where this is gonna go but what I can do is give you me, keep you safe while you walk on the wild side and work my ass off to do what I can so this never goes bad for you.”</i><br /><br />I'm totally sighing right now...<br /><br />Well, moving on. I think you lucked out, big time, when you found Tessa. She bakes, cooks, cleans, puts up with your family and she loves you and has your back. That is not so easy with your crazy family and even crazier job. Oh, and not to mention your ex. What did you see in her? You're a cop-you didn't see the entire time she was playing you, but you're supposed to be able to read killers? You may need to find yourself a different job, honey. <br /><br /><i>"He had that snow on him because he threw himself to the ground to dodge bullets aimed at him in front of my house.<br />My man had thrown his beautiful body to the snow to dodge fucking bullets aimed at him in front of my fucking house.<br />And he had his gun in his hand because he’d had to return fire.<br />And I knew exactly who ordered that unidentified male to aim bullets at my man.<br />No.<br />Oh no.<br />I did not fucking think so."</i><br /><br />She's also very protective of you. I did have a problem with her going to her abusive ex alone, in order to attack him. Love, she's a baker. How is that sane? Still, I forgive her because it was for you, and we all do crazy things for people we love. I was happy to see she fought off her attacker, but I found it hard to believe. Now tell me the truth, you gave her secret karate lessons. I'm right, right?<br /><br />Oh, and your boys, I just looooved them. I was so sad to see what they'd been through, but you raised them well. They will grow up and become men you'll be proud of. And, now they have Tessa to comfort them. <br /><br /><i>“When you were out running before we went to look at trucks that last Sunday you had them, I asked them to write a letter to Santa and they did,” I informed him.<br />“Babe, hate to break this to you but they’re ten and twelve. They know there’s no Santa Claus.”<br />I lifted my head and looked down at him. “Yeah, I know. But they aren’t stupid. They humored me because they also know I have a credit card.”</i><br /><br />And, I know you know this, but Tessa loves you a lot. She loves you for loving her and for being you. Being her Brock. And she knows exactly who her Brock is. Don't ever forget that.<br /><br /><i>“Brock Lucas is wild and he’s rough and he’s driven but he’s loving and affectionate and so fucking loyal it isn’t funny. He takes care of me. He makes me feel safe. He’s good through and through and that is the first and last fucking time I’ll listen to you talk shit about him."<br /><br />"He thought I was funny. He thought I was beautiful. He got close anytime I was near. He wanted to stand between me and roaring lions. He wanted to help me battle my ghosts. He had two fantastic sons, a screwy but loving family, a great body, an affectionate manner and he remembered the color of the nightie I wore our first night together in my bed."</i><br /><br />So, all in all, I think you two are the sweetest couple ever and I've enjoyed knowing you.<br /><br /><b>Love, Mimi</b><br /><br />P.S. What kind of nickname is Slim? You need something better.<br /><br />P.P.S. Just to spare you the effort of investigating how I know this, I admit:I'm your official stalker.<br /><br />P.P.P.S. You wouldn't be open to the idea of running away with me, right? I can't bake but I make mean pancakes. If not, have Tessa send me some cupcakes. Thanks in advance!<br /><br /> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/277975880" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 1 in the series</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/279263085" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 3 in the series</a><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/336327385" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for book 4 in the series</a></blockquote></span>

<div id="review_260917868" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260917868" />
    <a title="Nikki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5279570-nikki"><img alt="Nikki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423057450p2/5279570.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/260917868?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nikki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nikki" href="/user/show/5279570-nikki">Nikki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">KA addicts one and all.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=own-ebook">own-ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=kristen-ashley-why-so-awesome">kristen-ashley-why-so-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=4-and-a-half-stars">4-and-a-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=best-h-h-ever">best-h-h-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=perfect-heroine">perfect-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5279570-nikki?shelf=delicious-hero">delicious-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer260917868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7198785000931909376">4.5 stars.<br/><br/><i>Wild Man</i> had a different vibe to its predecessor <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_' title='Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mystery Man</a> but I've gotta say that I really, <b>really</b> enjoyed it. And no, not simply because it's another KA. It really touched me with its subtlety and I loved how it had such focus on Brock and Tess (H/h) and the solidity of their relationship. It also had lovely use of light and shade, there were cute kids in it (KA does GREAT kid) and when the characters spoke to each other it really meant something.<br/><br/>Brock was another hot alpha: protec</span>
  <span id="freeText7198785000931909376" style="display:none">4.5 stars.<br /><br /><i>Wild Man</i> had a different vibe to its predecessor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Mystery Man</a> but I've gotta say that I really, <b>really</b> enjoyed it. And no, not simply because it's another KA. It really touched me with its subtlety and I loved how it had such focus on Brock and Tess (H/h) and the solidity of their relationship. It also had lovely use of light and shade, there were cute kids in it (KA does GREAT kid) and when the characters spoke to each other it really meant something.<br /><br />Brock was another hot alpha: protective with a quick-to-ignite explosive streak, but gentle and loving and a family man through and through. Tess was ah-<i>muh</i>-zing: what you saw was what you got; no bullshit, no games, no over-the-top attitude (I had a serious girl crush on her the whole way through). Their passion for each other was intense, hot and left serious stars in my eyes. They were also totally honest with each other and I love when that happens in romance because it's so bloody refreshing to read.<blockquote>"I'm sorry, my reaction was selfish, I should have thought of you and I'll work on it but I'm a woman and women have this thing when their men have had women in their lives that are better looking than them. [...] You're hot. I should have known she would be beautiful but just how beautiful she is took me by surprise. Like I said, I'll work on that and try to get over it." [...]<br />When I stopped talking, Brock remained silent and stared up at me. [...] Then he asked, "You think Olivia is better looking than you?"<br />My brows drew together and I repeated, "Well... yeah." [...]<br />"Jesus, you haven't, have you?"<br />"I haven't what?"<br />"Ever played games."</blockquote>This was slower and steadier than the action packed, laugh a minute fun of <i>Mystery Man</i>. It focussed not only on Brock and Tess building a relationship but also the added influences of Brock's crazy, intrusive family, as well as <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Brock's darling sons, Joel and Rex, and his ongoing battle for custody of them against his bitchy-dreadful-mother of an ex <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and also Tess's hard work and success as a cake baking/decorating sensation.<br /><br />I don't know, I just loved it. It was honest and solid and so sweet.<blockquote>"[...] But all of that was worth it, all of it, since my reward is you." [...]<br />"Please, Brock, be quiet."<br />"No fuckin' way, baby," he whispered. "Today, I been thinkin' a lot about McManus and he lost his good one and there is no way I'm gonna find mine and not know right to my fuckin' bones she doesn't understand <i>precisely</i> what she means to me."</blockquote>Yep.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7198785000931909376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4365117-emily?shelf=starting-over-divorced-seperated">starting-over-divorced-seperated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4365117-emily?shelf=cover-red">cover-red</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4365117-emily?shelf=chef-baker">chef-baker</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer306696306" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16871747209272575874">It took years for Bakery owner Tessa O'Hara to be willing to try dating again, but the moment she sees Brock Lucas her hesitation goes out the window, he is the man for her. He has an edge to him that is undeniable, blunt way of speaking but there is a softness that overcomes him when he is with Tessa that has her feeling safer than he has ever felt in his life. After four months of dating she is ready to take the next step, but that idea is shattered when she finds out Brock is not who she thin</span>
  <span id="freeText16871747209272575874" style="display:none">It took years for Bakery owner Tessa O'Hara to be willing to try dating again, but the moment she sees Brock Lucas her hesitation goes out the window, he is the man for her. He has an edge to him that is undeniable, blunt way of speaking but there is a softness that overcomes him when he is with Tessa that has her feeling safer than he has ever felt in his life. After four months of dating she is ready to take the next step, but that idea is shattered when she finds out Brock is not who she thinks he is, he is an undercover DEA agent who was investigating her to see if she still had connections to her ex-husband.<br /><br />Even though Brock changed his name while with Tessa, everything he spoke about was true. He has given her time to seek him out, but after three months of her avoidance he has had enough, he wants her back. Convincing Tessa isn't as difficult as he thought, but as their new relationship moves forward hurdle after hurdle gets thrown there way, a crazy ex-wife whose jealousy has reared it's ugly head, an estranged member of the family fighting a terminal disease, and oh ya Tessa's ex won't leave her alone. <br /><br />**Reread, I have to say once I started this one I found that he reminded me a lot of Jaxson in Sons of Anarchy. Huge age difference but his demeanor is the same making it even more sizzling to read. This is one of my favorites for sure.<br /><br />I was torn with this one initially, I was so mad at Brock I was not sure he would be able to redeem himself, but he did. I don't know how Kristen Ashley does it, but this is the third book of hers I have read thus far and I am enamored by her talented ways of taking complicated characters and staying true to who they are through out the story. Brock has a temper, you get that from the beginning but somewhere along the way you accept it and realize it is who he is, no trying to change it, you deal with it. I thought this was another fantastic story, highly recommend.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16871747209272575874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1518913157" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10015714835282552549">This one I had to push myself to finish. In the end it worked out ok but I can say it's my least fave of all the KA I've read. It seems to go long in scenes that don't really move the plot forward. The connection between Tess and Brock doesn't seem as strong as the other couples. The plot is sensitive in nature in some areas but I don't think it really dove too deep. It just felt like both myself and the story were going through the motions without connecting. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156664469" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=fighters-and-bad-asses">fighters-and-bad-asses</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1156664469" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5780667241756167567"><b> 4 Wild Stars. </b>	<br/><br/>After a failed and abusive marriage, Tessa believes she’s finally free. She’s moved on, she has a job, a new life and even a new love interest. <br/>Until her ex-husband drags her to his world again with his obscure business making her being interviewed by the FBI. And that’s when she finds out that her new love interest is no one else but the detective responsible for her case, so as you can imagine she has trouble trusting him after she finds out. <br/>But now that Brock got her, he will</span>
  <span id="freeText5780667241756167567" style="display:none"><b> 4 Wild Stars. </b>	<br><br>After a failed and abusive marriage, Tessa believes she’s finally free. She’s moved on, she has a job, a new life and even a new love interest. <br>Until her ex-husband drags her to his world again with his obscure business making her being interviewed by the FBI. And that’s when she finds out that her new love interest is no one else but the detective responsible for her case, so as you can imagine she has trouble trusting him after she finds out. <br>But now that Brock got her, he will do everything to have her. The fact that she stills needs protection is just the perfect excuse for him to not leave her alone and get her for good in the process. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468447640i/19708031.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, there’s not much to say about this book besides that it’s another Kristen Ashley win, I mean, there’s a reason why she is the romance queen, right? <br>One sexy alpha hero, a sweet heroine, a bunch of great supportive characters, sexy moments and lots of action/drama… seriously, what’s not to love? <br>I didn’t like it as much as the first one (mainly because of Hawk), but it was a damn good book. And the best thing? Knowing that even having read a lot of KA books… I still have a looooong way to go. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429744792i/14626262.jpg" width="350" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Abusive ex-husband.
