<div id="review_416874581" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/416874581" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416874581?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416874581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16054259228470729994">Wow!! What a great book!! I was entertained from start to finish with this one! This is my third Kristen Ashley book, and I have got to say that I LOVE her alpha males! There is just something so realistic and heart warming about them. Brock Lucas aka "Slim" is pure alpha-male from his head all the way down to his toes. He is in law enforcement, and is first introduced to Tessa O'Hara while undercover as a guy named Jake. This is how Tessa knows him for the first four months of their "relationsh</span>
  <span id="freeText16054259228470729994" style="display:none">Wow!! What a great book!! I was entertained from start to finish with this one! This is my third Kristen Ashley book, and I have got to say that I LOVE her alpha males! There is just something so realistic and heart warming about them. Brock Lucas aka "Slim" is pure alpha-male from his head all the way down to his toes. He is in law enforcement, and is first introduced to Tessa O'Hara while undercover as a guy named Jake. This is how Tessa knows him for the first four months of their "relationship." When she finds out the truth, she feels betrayed and walks of into the sunset!<br />After Brock gives her time to simmer down..( try 3 months!) he pushes his way back into her life wanting to continue where they left off, only this time with her knowing the "real" him. Tessa gives into him; which, in my opinion she should have made him grovel..ALOT!!!She doesn't though and she takes him back and the rest is smooth sailing...NOT!! There is so much that goes down for this poor couple, it is amazing they have anytime to even look at one another. From crazy exes, to family problems, and even gunshots around their home; there is literally never a dull moment. One thing is for sure though, these two grow to love each other very much, and what I adore about the both of them is their loyalty to one another, as well as their family and friends. Tessa, is a sweetheart and it is just plain hard to find anything negative about her. She is so easy going, and yet, when the chips are down, she will fight like a tiger to protect the ones she loves. Brock is more rougher around the edges, but he has a protective streak a mile wide and he is as loyal as they come. Brock is someone you would want to have at your back when the world is fallen apart around you. I loved everything about these two as a couple, they just seemed to work so well together, and what you see is what you get with them. There were no games played between them.<br />The sex for me, was just ok.. I would have liked a little more steam in the bedroom. Also, one thing I am still getting used to in a KA book, is the "lingo". Her way of writing is different than most, and I find sometimes I am scrambling to understand what is being said. Other than that, I have no complaints about this book. It was a wonderful journey of two people who have fallen in love!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16054259228470729994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16044807471450595507"><b> 5 Still Has The Power Stars<br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>I have been re-visiting my KA reads of the Dream Man Series. This book held up to the power of Brock and all that was him. What was impressive was the strength and smarts of Tess. The way these two were a single unit once they got straightened out from their first go around to what they became was a lesson in what loving another person should be. </b><br/><br/>These were grown people and they knew when they found their person, to hold on and power through the </span>
  <span id="freeText16044807471450595507" style="display:none"><b> 5 Still Has The Power Stars<br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>I have been re-visiting my KA reads of the Dream Man Series. This book held up to the power of Brock and all that was him. What was impressive was the strength and smarts of Tess. The way these two were a single unit once they got straightened out from their first go around to what they became was a lesson in what loving another person should be. </b><br><br>These were grown people and they knew when they found their person, to hold on and power through the bad stuff for the good. I especially appreciated their relationship was based on no lies or game playing. It all just worked.<br><br>Side note... I think Brock was a path for KA in her working out Tack for Motorcycle Man. Yes, Tack already was part of other books... but Brock comes pretty close to a lot of Tack in his ways to me. I could be totally off base...but that came to me while reading this. <br><br>So the question for me is... do I go back to the beginning and do Mystery Man again...or just jump to Tack's Story... as that was a true 5 star for me.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer17738778157389420603">5 Bonafide KA LOVER STARS!!!!<br/><br/>(BR with Melissa, Denisse, Elizabeth, Shannon, Tiffany, Angie, Anne & Bridgid)<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zpsa2b8272e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392523958i/8573218._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zpsa2b8272e.jpg' height='400' width='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This is my second KA book and I've got to say, I believe I'm sold on KA's awesomeness!!<br/><br/>Wild Man is the story of Brock Lucas (aka Jake Knox) and Tess O'Hara.<br/>Where do I begin to tell just how much I loved this story and what was it that made me love it so much??!!!<br/><br/>First, the heroine and Alpha, are both over 40!!<br/>Over 40, and HOT as HELL!!!!!<br/>Brock Lucas is all ALPHA. <br/>From HEAD TO TOE.<br/>He's g</span>
  <span id="freeText17738778157389420603" style="display:none">5 Bonafide KA LOVER STARS!!!!<br><br>(BR with Melissa, Denisse, Elizabeth, Shannon, Tiffany, Angie, Anne &amp; Bridgid)<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zpsa2b8272e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>This is my second KA book and I've got to say, I believe I'm sold on KA's awesomeness!!<br><br>Wild Man is the story of Brock Lucas (aka Jake Knox) and Tess O'Hara.<br>Where do I begin to tell just how much I loved this story and what was it that made me love it so much??!!!<br><br>First, the heroine and Alpha, are both over 40!!<br>Over 40, and HOT as HELL!!!!!<br>Brock Lucas is all ALPHA. <br>From HEAD TO TOE.<br>He's got a dirty, smutty mouth, and he knows how to use it, among other parts of his body as well. ;)<br>Tess, well, she is FANTASTIC!!<br>I FREAKIN' LOVED HER HARD!!!!!<br>This woman is definitely a book heroine that I want to be BFFs with!!<br>She was never annoying throughout the story and I'd say she was actually "KICK-ASS"!!!<br>AND, she can bake a mean Carrot Cake!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps89f484f9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392523958i/8573219._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps89f484f9.jpg" height="350" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>We met Brock briefly in "Mystery Man".<br>He was the undercover DEA agent that was doing Darla to get to the leader of a drug ring. <br><br>In the story, he's undercover, again, but as "Jake Knox", the man dating Tess, but with the purpose of getting to her ex husband, Damian Heller, who also has known ties to some unsavory people.<br><br>Soon, Tess learns of Brock's true identity and they quickly sort things out.<br>Brock may have been undercover but his feelings were 100% true for Tess, and he wasn't going to let her go.<br><br>These two were perfect!!<br>I loved that neither played games with the other!!<br>The sex was oh so panty soaking hot and Brock, well this guy didn't seem to need a break in between love making sessions to gain his strength back.<br>This guy had the libido of the freakin' energizer bunny!! <br><br>Brock and Tess, both have horrible ex's to deal with.<br>Tess suffered terribly at the hands of her ex.<br>Brock's ex wife was pretty much a sorry excuse for a human being and she never hesitated to manipulate their two little boys whenever she felt the urge.<br><br>There's one part where Olivia shows up at Tess's bakery and man I wanted to leap into the book and smack a bitch!!!<br>Oh and this is one of my favorite parts in the story as well.<br>Tess is truly a class act!!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/bring-it-on-bitch_zpsd3a71ae1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392523958ra/8573220.gif" alt=" photo bring-it-on-bitch_zpsd3a71ae1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Olivia tries so many times to get in between Brock and Tess, but Brock doesn't fall for any of her stupid ploys to get his attention.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/PrH6qaH_zpsd61da7bd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392523958ra/8573221.gif" alt=" photo PrH6qaH_zpsd61da7bd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Dade McManus, Olivia's current husband, was amazing, and most of the gals in our buddy read agreed.<br>How Olivia got so lucky and married two amazing men, is beyond me!!<br><br><br>I'd say that at this moment, Brock is my favorite KA Alpha!!<br>The man isn't filthy stinkin' rich and he may have a really dirty mouth but he is a man of his word and he does whatever he can to protect his woman, AND, he NEVER disappoints in the bedroom!! WHOA...Fanning myself!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_mqcy46kSvr1sv2uawo1_500_zpsd9883f33.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389425791ra/8030252.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mqcy46kSvr1sv2uawo1_500_zpsd9883f33.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Tess, at the age of 43, has never had children of her own, and now is unable to, but she takes to Joel and Rex as if they were her own.<br>I loved the relationship that developed between her and the boys.<br>Tess is all sweetness, but if anyone threatens the people she loves or her wonderful life she has built with Brock, she fights with such a fierceness. <br>She is no weak damsel in distress!!<br><br>There are a ton of really memorable secondary characters and some faves from "Mystery Man" in this story!<br><br>The epilogue tugged at my heart strings.<br><br>I've noticed so far, that KA knows how to create an ALPHA and she gives us heroines that are so lovable!!<br>Heroines usually fall short for me, but Tess, she might be my fave as of this moment!<br><br>What an amazing story and I'm so happy I got to experience it with a bunch of really awesome ladies!!<br>I haven't laughed so hard during a buddy read, ever!!!<br><br>Can't wait to start "Law Man" with this lovely group!!!!<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I'm like all women. You see this but inside there's something else that I won't let you see or him see but it's the mess he left me. But that's mine. No one gets to it. Everything you get and he gets is a show. One thing you learn really quickly and really well when that kind of thing happens to you is to be a fucking great actress."</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"Tess, babe, eyes,"</b>
</i> <b>he growled.</b> <i>
  <b>"Now."</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I can't make any promises about where this is gonna go but what I can do is give you me, keep you safe while you walk on the wild side and work my ass off to do what I can so this never goes bad for you."</b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>"Babe, you think I found the woman of my dreams at forty-five years old and I'm gonna let anything happen to her, think again. That's a long fuckin' time to wait for what you want. I waited. I found it. I'm pullin' out all the stops to take care of it. I know you feel the same for me so I'm doin' the same to keep me safe for you."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><br></span>

Sorry my friends, but I couldn't invite anybody to the weeding because it all happened so fast, and you all know how demanding those Alpha males can be.   <span id="freeText12690780111193351803" style="display:none"><b>******10+ Wild Stars *****</b><br><br>Loved, loved, adore this book, so much in fact, that I became Mrs. Brock Lucas. Sorry my friends, but I couldn't invite anybody to the weeding because it all happened so fast, and you all know how demanding those Alpha males can be. LOL!!!<br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/279c712019a437bf577c4b341d2102ee_zpsf9f76113.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>When Brock Lucas met Tess O'Hara it was not under the ideal circumstances but he knew right away he wanted to taste and keep the sweet she had in her and Tess just melted once she look into those silver eyes. Brock is a DEA agent investigating a crime and Tess is a bakery owner with one awful Ex husband who keeps showing up even though She has made it very clear that she's done with him. Brock is wild and Tess is sweet, both have had difficult pasts but they were quick to realized that they wanted to be together and will not allow anything or anybody to come between them.<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/49735f3efe31abd6fa31d83784d09f06_zps25cfa23e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>My man Brock is the definition of sexy and wild, this man has it going on and I just fell instantly in love with him. I must admit though that Tess was one cool chick too, she was the perfect partner for Brock, no games, no lies. Totally refreshing to read a story were the characters were confident in each other and in their love not to be playing around and creating stupid drama. Now, don't go thinking this book was boring or that it didn't have action, because there was plenty of that, both Brock's and Tess's exes were a pain in the neck and they provided with more drama than I can tell you. <br>This book was super fun, super sexy and it just solidified my love for Kristen Ashley's writing, she is s a mastermind of creating Alpha Males and sexy loves stories.<br>What put the cherry on top my sundae or the sprinkles on my cupcake was the fabulous experience that was reading this book with my girls <i>Patty, Melissa, Shannon, Elizabeth and Tiffany</i>, it was so much fun to share this read with them and laugh and be naughty together and I can't wait to do it again...<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10870011009150505180">I liked this a lot, but as far as Kristen Ashley's books go, it wasn't a favorite. I'm not sure why, but it didn't hold my attention the way her books normally do. I liked Brock and Tess as a couple, I liked Brock's kids and his zany family, and I <b>LOVED</b> Tess's bakery. I would consider Tess's cakes a main character in this book. I ate more than my usual share of sweets while I was reading this!! <br/><br/>So overall, a very good read, just not as good or as memorable as most of her other books. The very go</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7059968352826631413">(5 "Hard not to love Tess" Stars)<br/>(BR with Patty, Denisse, Tiffany, Elizabeth, Angie, Anne, Shannon & Bridgid)<br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/2216e388-18cd-4726-8eef-31ff1add5e57.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/3658c239-9bb7-4820-8c84-acba0ad3abb5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Tessa O'Hara aka Tess/sweetness, is a 43 year old, divorced woman who owns a bakery called Tessa's Cakes. Tess wasted most of her adult life being the wife of an abusive man. Once free from him, Tess just wants a fresh start. She is working in her bakery one day, and a hot man walks in that takes her breath away! He ends up asking her out. She accepts, and is instantly captivated </span>
  <span id="freeText7059968352826631413" style="display:none">(5 "Hard not to love Tess" Stars)<br>(BR with Patty, Denisse, Tiffany, Elizabeth, Angie, Anne, Shannon &amp; Bridgid)<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/2216e388-18cd-4726-8eef-31ff1add5e57.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392239037i/8524145.jpg" alt=" photo 2216e388-18cd-4726-8eef-31ff1add5e57.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/3658c239-9bb7-4820-8c84-acba0ad3abb5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392494047i/8569193._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 3658c239-9bb7-4820-8c84-acba0ad3abb5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tessa O'Hara aka Tess/sweetness, is a 43 year old, divorced woman who owns a bakery called Tessa's Cakes. Tess wasted most of her adult life being the wife of an abusive man. Once free from him, Tess just wants a fresh start. She is working in her bakery one day, and a hot man walks in that takes her breath away! He ends up asking her out. She accepts, and is instantly captivated and hooked on him.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/8fcaacea-7da6-478d-a0e5-657fcd2b4931.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487278i/8568237._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8fcaacea-7da6-478d-a0e5-657fcd2b4931.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brock Lucas aka slim/honey is a 45 year old man who works as a DEA agent. He is extremely committed to his job, and taking out the bad guys. His latest job involves Tess's ex-husband. He gets close to Tess because of his case, but things quickly turn real.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/a88921a3-ea58-47bc-88cc-421c7a078c3e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392492946i/8569116.jpg" alt=" photo a88921a3-ea58-47bc-88cc-421c7a078c3e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brock hasn't had much luck in his past relationships either, and finds Tess refreshing. He loves she doesn't play games, and that what you see is what you get. They have been dating for four months when Tess finds out that the man she knows as Jake Knox is really Brock Lucas. They struggle with the lies, and work to trust each other. They deal with ex's, family drama, and really open up to each other about their past. <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/8f49ba8b-6129-4b0b-9452-edea755d0061.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487278i/8568238._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8f49ba8b-6129-4b0b-9452-edea755d0061.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really enjoyed this book &amp; thought the female lead was fabulous! Kristen Ashley continues to wow me with her amazing sexy, beautiful alpha men! Sexy time with Brock was just delicious, but I also found myself wanting me some Levi! Would love a book for Levi too! I think he definitely has Dream Man potential! :D <br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/93177613-5921-4872-926c-72bc2dd50ccc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392494229i/8569210.jpg" alt=" photo 93177613-5921-4872-926c-72bc2dd50ccc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-And I knew, feeling the burn of his eyes, what that look meant. I knew this man, this fantastic, striking, wild man, was mine.<br><br>-"You know what's goin' down with you and me. You know what you feel when I kiss you.<br><br>-"I'm also lucky my girl had a craving to take a walk on the wild side," he muttered, his quicksilver eyes dropping to my mouth.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/36209228-ae60-4ef3-ae56-74a30fa1c98e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487278i/8568239.jpg" alt=" photo 36209228-ae60-4ef3-ae56-74a30fa1c98e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-His eyelids got heavy, his arms got tighter, my arms around him got tighter, his head descended, and he kissed me again, this time longer, deeper, sweeter, and even more delicious.<br><br>-You are the only woman I know who doesn't need words. Everything you do speaks for you and it never lies. Just your hand on me, babe, said it all."<br><br>-It was wild. It was heated. It was energetic. There was a lot of rolling, groping, tongues, teeth, fingers, moans, groans, whimpers, sighs, and gasps as he took, I took, he gave, and I gave.<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/a686fc33-a5f5-473f-a2b9-1d583517608c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392494229i/8569211.jpg" alt=" photo a686fc33-a5f5-473f-a2b9-1d583517608c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-Sliding my hand down his throat then farther to explore the sleek, solid wall of his chest, I held his heated, mercury eyes and whispered, "God, honey, you're so fucking beautiful."<br><br>-"Brock Lucas is wild and he's rough and he's driven but he's loving and affectionate and so fucking loyal it isn't funny. He takes care of me. He makes me feel safe.<br><br>-"You're wrong, darlin'. I got wild in me. And I'll never lose it. It's just that my wild is a safe place for you and it always will be."<br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/f24ac41d-ee61-4cf2-8fcf-e3e3c866e9c6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487278i/8568240.jpg" alt=" photo f24ac41d-ee61-4cf2-8fcf-e3e3c866e9c6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s993.photobucket.com/user/dalaa158/media/5f3e8816-b943-473e-9a8e-47de09c90830.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392487278i/8568241.jpg" alt=" photo 5f3e8816-b943-473e-9a8e-47de09c90830.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_17375956'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17375956-reaper-s-property"><img alt="Reaper&#39;s Property (Reapers MC, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1360943604l/17375956._SY160_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MtDtkGx/A5Y024xAab9tC0aHhArT0Jbr8Fm14LA9GEGGzE8NCnVtwSI6RqV9riCcb2FDXjKcXUOIYeHKjenZAw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OTgT6+/TwbvtRhtkLyh9WpT/B2kSDa3sB1wG6zVN+uyNJLF2idmv7Pun0YE7OTDNvRnAPfNBZkR/ZFLBCJk7rg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer1557959744645835646">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText1557959744645835646" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
